## gateway_isolation
  [PASS] no_gateway_in_lib: lib crates must not have a gateway/ directory â€” gateway belongs in gateway-type crates

## hygiene
  [PASS] embed_config_needs_override: include_str! embedding a config file must be paired with a runtime read â€” use embed as fallback, not sole source
  [PASS] no_allow_dead_code: Source files must not suppress the dead_code lint via #[allow(dead_code)] or #[expect(dead_code)] â€” dead code in production layers is a defect signal, not something to silence
  [PASS] no_allow_unused_imports: Source files must not suppress the unused_imports lint via #[allow(unused_imports)]
  [PASS] no_bare_expect: No bare .expect() with empty or placeholder message
  [PASS] no_bare_unwrap: No bare .unwrap() calls in production source
  [PASS] no_hardcoded_home_paths: No hardcoded home directory paths in source code
  [PASS] no_panic_in_lib: No panic!() in library code
  [PASS] no_println_in_library_code: Library code must not use println!/eprintln! â€” use tracing macros (info!, warn!, error!) instead
  [PASS] no_stub_fn_bodies: Production functions must not have stub bodies (todo!(), unimplemented!(), or empty)
  [PASS] no_unused_deps: Dependencies declared in Cargo.toml must be used in main/src/
  [PASS] no_weak_fs_patterns: Weak filesystem patterns â€” code that produces host-dependent paths (MAIN_SEPARATOR, hardcoded \\, replace-hacks, literal backslashes)
  [PASS] xdg_dirs_crate: CLI projects should use dirs/directories crate for XDG-compliant paths

## interface
  [PASS] api_no_core_import: api/ layer must not import from core/ (L2 must not depend on L3)
  [PASS] api_no_factory_trait: pub traits named *Factory must not appear in api/ â€” Factory traits are static constructor namespaces, not port contracts, and cannot be used as dyn Trait
  [PASS] api_no_gateway_dep: api/ must not import from gateway/ â€” api/ defines abstractions, it must not depend on implementations
  [PASS] api_no_spi_dep: api/ must not import from spi/ â€” api/ defines abstractions, it must not depend on implementations
  [PASS] api_trait_must_be_object_safe: pub traits in api/ with methods must declare at least one self receiver â€” static-only traits are non-object-safe and provide no runtime abstraction
  [PASS] boundary_cargo_cross_level: L2 domain primitives must not depend on L3+ assembler-layer workspace members â€” declare workspace_level in [package.metadata.struct-engine] to enable
  [PASS] boundary_l2_no_l3_import: L2 must not import from L3 (core/ and spi/ must not depend on saf/)
  [PASS] boundary_l2_no_l4_import: L2 must not import from L4 (core/ and spi/ must not depend on gateway/)
  [PASS] boundary_peer_isolation: L2 peers must not import each other (core/ â†› spi/, spi/ â†› core/)
  [PASS] config_methods_pub_crate: Config struct methods must be pub(crate), not pub â€” configs are not for public consumption
  [PASS] deprecated_trait_usage: Reports deprecated trait definitions in api/traits.rs for tracking
  [PASS] error_types_in_api: Error types that cross layer boundaries must be declared in api/, not in core/
  [PASS] gateway_no_core_dep: gateway/ must not import from core/ â€” gateway/ calls saf/, not core/ directly
  [PASS] gateway_no_spi_dep: gateway/ must not import from spi/ â€” gateway/ depends on saf/ only, not on SPI implementations
  [PASS] layers_no_free_standing_fn: SEA layer files must not contain free-standing fn â€” all functions must be methods on a type (OOP violation)
  [PASS] lib_no_pub_mod_api: lib.rs must not declare api as public (pub mod api is forbidden â€” all layers must be private)
  [PASS] lib_no_pub_mod_core: lib.rs must not declare core as public (pub mod core is forbidden)
  [CORE/SPI:L2] [PASS] no_traits_in_impl_layer: L2 layers must not define traits (implementations only â€” traits belong in L1/api)
  [PASS] pub_types_in_api_only: All public types (struct, enum, trait, type alias) must be declared under api/ â€” no other layer is a legal declaration site
  [PASS] saf_no_core_import: saf/ must not import from core/ â€” saf/ composes via api/ and spi/ only; any use of crate::core:: in saf/ couples the facade to implementation details
  [PASS] saf_no_core_reexport: saf/ must not re-export from core/ (SAF re-exports from api/ and spi/ only)
  [PASS] saf_no_gateway_dep: saf/ must not import from gateway/ â€” gateway/ calls saf/, not the reverse
  [PASS] saf_no_pub_struct: saf/ must not define new pub structs (facade layer only re-exports and wires)
  [PASS] saf_no_trait_reexport: saf/ must not re-export traits via pub use â€” this applies to both internal api/traits re-exports and external crate SPI extension points (Scheduler, Broker, Stream, Executor, Worker, Listener, etc.); wrap trait methods as standalone functions instead
  [PASS] sea_api_no_core_dep: api/ must not import from core/ â€” api/ defines abstractions, it must not depend on implementations
  [PASS] sea_layers_no_crates: SEA layer directories must not contain crates (no Cargo.toml inside api/, core/, saf/, spi/)

## mod
  [PASS] mod_rs_not_reexport_shim: SEA layer mod.rs must not be a crate-level re-export shim
  [PASS] module_entry_declarations_only: mod.rs must contain only module declarations and re-exports â€” no struct/impl/fn logic
  [FAIL] saf_mod_no_api_direct_reexport: saf/mod.rs and saf/<theme>/mod.rs must not contain pub use crate::api:: â€” all api/ re-exports must flow through a _svc.rs file (1 offender)
    -> main\src\saf\domain\mod.rs: main\src\saf\domain\mod.rs:14: saf/mod.rs contains direct api/ re-export â€” `pub use crate::api::Domain;` must be moved to a _svc.rs file
       Fix: Move the pub use crate::api:: re-export into the corresponding <trait>_svc.rs file; saf/mod.rs must only declare submodules and re-export from them

## naming
  [PASS] api_filename_matches_type: Each pub type/trait in api/ must be in its own standalone file with the file stem matching the snake_case name
  [PASS] api_no_default_prefix: api/ files and types must not use the Default* prefix â€” Default* names signal a concrete implementation variant that belongs in core/, not in the contract layer
  [PASS] bin_names_valid: Binary names use hyphens or underscores
  [PASS] cargo_pkg_name_kebab_case: Package name uses kebab-case
  [PASS] config_file_to_builder_naming: Config files must map to corresponding ConfigBuilder struct names: <name>.toml â†’ <Name>ConfigBuilder
  [PASS] folder_names_snake_case: Directory names under main/src/ must use snake_case
  [PASS] layer_module_no_underscore: SEA layer directory names must not contain underscores â€” use nested directories instead of underscore-concatenated names
  [PASS] module_name_not_prefix_type: Module name must not prefix the struct/trait name (e.g., config::Config not config::ConfigConfig)
  [PASS] module_names_match: Module file names match mod declarations
  [PASS] module_names_no_stutter: Module and file names under src/ must not stutter: the first snake_case token must not equal the last
  [PASS] no_default_suffix: struct and enum names must not end with the Default suffix â€” the Default* prefix (DefaultValidator) is the reserved convention for the standard implementation variant; the *Default suffix (ValidatorDefault) is the ambiguous mirror
  [PASS] package_name_no_sea_suffix: Package name must not use SEA layer suffixes as defined in sea_layers config
  [PASS] rs_files_no_uppercase: No uppercase in source file names
  [PASS] rs_files_snake_case: Source files use snake_case naming
  [PASS] suggest_builder_pattern: Suggest Builder pattern for complex structs (advisory)
  [PASS] trait_names_not_plural: Trait names must be singular (not plural)

## oop
  [PASS] api_facade_hides_core: api/ types must not expose internal core/ implementation in their public API signatures
  [PASS] api_no_pub_enum: Enums in api/ must follow same privacy rules as structs â€” not bare pub unless explicitly documented
  [PASS] core_no_bare_pub_fn: Functions in core/ must use pub(crate) instead of bare pub â€” core/ is not part of the public API
  [PASS] no_type_alias_leaks_impl: Type aliases in api/ must not expose internal impl details (core/ types, private generics) â€” use newtypes or abstract trait types instead

## saf
  [PASS] lib_delegates_to_saf: lib.rs must delegate public surface to saf/ via pub use
  [PASS] saf_free_fn_takes_local_type: Free functions in saf/ or core/ taking an api-defined type as parameter should be methods on that type
  [PASS] saf_mod_exists: saf/mod.rs must exist (SAF facade entry point)
  [PASS] saf_no_wrapper_methods: saf/ methods must not be thin wrappers â€” a saf/ method whose entire body delegates to a free function or another method adds no value and signals incomplete consolidation
  [PASS] saf_returns_api_types: saf/ pub fn return types must be declared in api/types/ (when spi/ is absent)
  [PASS] saf_signature_no_core_types: saf/ public function signatures must not name types from core/ (signature leak)
  [PASS] saf_svc_returns: saf/ public function return types depend on crate extensibility: if spi/ exists, return `impl Trait` for downstream polymorphism; if spi/ does not exist, return concrete types only (no trait leaks)

## saf_svc
  [PASS] api_trait_fn_scenario_coverage: Every fn in a pub trait in api/ must have _happy, _error, and _edge test coverage in tests/
  [PASS] saf_no_env_reads: saf/ must not read environment variables directly â€” env access is domain logic and belongs in core/
  [PASS] saf_svc_single_trait_surface: Each _svc.rs in saf/ must only re-export from api/ â€” pub use from core:: leaks implementation details
  [PASS] saf_trait_svc_correspondence: Every pub trait in api/ must have a corresponding <trait_snake>_svc.rs in saf/
  [PASS] saf_trait_svc_fn_scenario_coverage: Every _svc.rs must have at least one pub item; every pub fn must have _happy, _error, and _edge test coverage
  [PASS] saf_trait_svc_test_exists: Each <trait>_svc.rs in saf/ must have a corresponding test file in tests/

## security
  [PASS] security_dependency_audit_configured: Project must configure dependency vulnerability auditing via deny.toml or cargo audit in CI
  [PASS] security_no_hardcoded_secrets: Source files must not contain hardcoded secrets, credentials, or API keys
  [PASS] security_policy_file_exists: Project must have a security policy file (SECURITY.md, SECURITY.txt, or .github/SECURITY.md)
  [PASS] security_unsafe_documented: Every unsafe block must be preceded by a // SAFETY: comment explaining the invariant

## service_type
  [PASS] service_type_core_implements_trait: core/ must implement the primary api trait (impl <PrimaryTrait> for)
  [PASS] service_type_defined: service_type must be defined in project metadata
  [PASS] service_type_has_validator: Every non-orchestrator crate must have a Validator trait in api/traits.rs
  [PASS] service_type_primary_trait_exists: api/traits.rs must contain the primary trait matching service_type

## shim_detection
  [PASS] lib_path_inside_src: [lib] and [[bin]] paths must point inside main/src/
  [PASS] lib_rs_not_shim: lib.rs must be a real entry point, not a shim with only re-exports
  [PASS] sea_layer_min_loc: SEA layer directories must meet minimum LOC threshold (api/>10, core/>20, saf/>5)
  [PASS] sea_layer_substantive_code: SEA layer files must contain substantive code (not just comments or empty re-exports)
  [PASS] structural_checks_match_lib_path: Non-standard [lib] path with main/src/ present suggests shim directory

## spi
  [PASS] spi_dir_not_empty: spi must be a directory (main/src/spi/mod.rs) with real code â€” a flat main/src/spi.rs file or an empty/comment-only main/src/spi/mod.rs is invalid SEA structure
  [PASS] spi_private_mod_in_lib: When spi/ exists, lib.rs must declare `mod spi` (private, not pub mod)
